Brought my car in to get my front end repaired on my Scion. The work was done very well. The repairs almost appear seamless. The paint work is spot on for a rare factory color my car came in. I really admire the work. For the next few weeks upon picking up my car I noticed some horrible repairs under the surfaces. Unnecessary screws holding panels where screws never were from the factory; just to keep things together. Really choppy/lazy approach to quick repairs. What gets me most about my experience with this shop is from the beginning of the whole process. The first day when I brought in my car, with an appointment and all, the service adviser that will be taking care of my car wasn't even there. Though the whole process of my car being in this shop I've been passed from advisor to another advisor. A total of four advisors and none have ever updated me on the status of my vehicle. I work for Honda so I know how most service centers work but this shop is just absurd when it comes to customer notifications. The worst part of the whole service is my GoPro that I use as a dash cam was TAKEN/STOLEN. I know it was taken because I stash the camera under my drivers seat out of sight and in a compartment which holds a vehicle lift/jack set. it doesn't stop there. The I mentioned the problem with the last service advisor who helped me and he told me to send an invoice. I've sent countless emails and called so many times I lost count. NO REPLY AT ALL. (Even emailed corporate with no response.)
It's just a shame since the Honda I work for we refer our customers to numerous Service Kings in the South Bay. Obviously I will no longer refer our customers to this location. (Should have known the reputation CARWEST had in the past before it became Service King.)
I was initially going to rate this service center 3 stars because I love the work that was done but upon writing this review I was just reminded of all the problems I've been though and my Stolen Camera.

If you ever decide to do business with this shop. Be very Cautious. Good Luck.<//Review>

< text>
I go here almost every friday for the Tuna deal they have. Its the closest from my work and easy to deal with since you can order through the app. Most times ive picked up through the app there were things off about the sandwich (ill get extra ingredients or things are missing, the directions werent followed as closely etc). Today, Jasmine did my order, and it was a great sandwich. Her attention to detail was on spot and she even wrapped my sandwich twice without requesting (never even thought of that. I always have a problem with the juices leaking over time). In general this place is pretty good and their indoor facility is clean and usually quick when they are a little busy. I dont expect perfection with the app orders most times anyway but Jasmine really went above and beyond today.<//text>
